    28	// POST /api/transactions/create - Create transaction and initiate payment
    29	async function postHandler(req: NextRequest) {
    30	  const startTime = Date.now();
    31	  // Extract client info for storing in transaction
    32	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    33	
    34	  try {
    35	    const session = await getServerSession(authOptions);
    36	    const body = await req.json();
    37	    const { items, shippingInfo, paymentMethod, promoCode } = body;
    38	
    39	    log.info('Transaction creation started', {
    40	      userId: session?.user?.id || 'guest',
    41	      itemCount: items?.length || 0,
    42	      paymentMethod: paymentMethod || 'STRIPE',
    43	      ip:
    44	        req.headers.get('x-forwarded-for') ||
    45	        req.headers.get('x-real-ip') ||
    46	        'unknown',
    47	    });
    48	
    49	    // Validate items
    50	    if (!items || !Array.isArray(items) || items.length === 0) {
    51	      return NextResponse.json(
    52	        { error: 'Your cart is empty.' },
    53	        { status: 400 }
    54	      );
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    for (const item of items) {
    58	      if (!item || typeof item.productId !== 'string' || !item.productId) {
    59	        return NextResponse.json(
    60	          { error: 'Cart items are invalid.' },
    61	          { status: 400 }
    62	        );
    63	      }
    64	
    65	      if (
    66	        item.variantId !== undefined &&
    67	        item.variantId !== null &&
    68	        typeof item.variantId !== 'string'
    69	      ) {
    70	        return NextResponse.json(
    71	          { error: 'Variant id is invalid.' },
    72	          { status: 400 }
    73	        );
    74	      }
    75	
    76	      const quantity = Number(item.quantity);
    77	      if (!Number.isInteger(quantity) || quantity <= 0) {
    78	        return NextResponse.json(
    79	          { error: 'Quantity must be a positive whole number.' },
    80	          { status: 400 }
    81	        );
    82	      }
    83	
    84	      item.quantity = quantity;
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    // Validate shipping info
    88	    if (!shippingInfo) {
    89	      return NextResponse.json(
    90	        { error: 'Shipping information is required.' },
    91	        { status: 400 }
    92	      );
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    // For logged-in users, merge profile data with form data
    96	    // Use profile data for non-null fields, allow form data to fill in null fields
    97	    let finalFullName: string;
    98	    let finalPhone: string;
    99	    let finalEmail: string | undefined;
   100	    let shouldUpdateProfile = false;
   101	
   102	    if (session?.user) {
   103	      // Use session data (already fresh from NextAuth)
   104	      const { fullName, phone, email } = shippingInfo;
   105	
   106	      // For logged-in users: Use session data if available, otherwise allow form data
   107	      // Priority: Session data > Form data > Error for required fields
   108	      finalFullName = session.user.name || fullName || '';
   109	      finalPhone = session.user.phone || phone || '';
   110	      finalEmail = session.user.email || email || undefined;
   111	
   112	      // Validate required fields
   113	      if (!finalFullName) {
   114	        return NextResponse.json(
   115	          { error: 'Please enter your full name.' },
   116	          { status: 400 }
   117	        );
   118	      }
   119	
   120	      if (!finalPhone) {
   121	        return NextResponse.json(
   122	          { error: 'Please enter your phone number.' },
   123	          { status: 400 }
   124	        );
   125	      }
   126	
   127	      // Check if we need to update profile with new values from form
   128	      if (!session.user.name && fullName) {
   129	        shouldUpdateProfile = true;
   130	      }
   131	      if (!session.user.phone && phone) {
   132	        shouldUpdateProfile = true;
   133	      }
   134	      if (!session.user.email && email) {
   135	        shouldUpdateProfile = true;
   136	      }
   137	
   138	      log.info('Using merged user data for transaction', {
   139	        userId: session.user.id,
   140	        finalPhone,
   141	        finalEmail,
   142	        fromProfile: {
   143	          name: !!session.user.name,
   144	          phone: !!session.user.phone,
   145	          email: !!session.user.email,
   146	        },
   147	        fromForm: {
   148	          name: !session.user.name && !!fullName,
   149	          phone: !session.user.phone && !!phone,
   150	          email: !session.user.email && !!email,
   151	        },
   152	        willUpdateProfile: shouldUpdateProfile,
   153	      });
   154	    } else {
   155	      // For guest users, use form data
   156	      const { fullName, phone, email } = shippingInfo;
   157	
   158	      if (!fullName || !phone) {
   159	        return NextResponse.json(
   160	          { error: 'Please complete all required fields.' },
   161	          { status: 400 }
   162	        );
   163	      }
   164	
   165	      finalFullName = fullName;
   166	      finalPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
   167	      finalEmail = email || undefined;
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    // Validate shipping address (both logged-in and guest users)
   171	    const { shippingAddress, postalCode, createAccount } = shippingInfo;
   172	
   173	    if (!shippingAddress) {
   174	      return NextResponse.json(
   175	        { error: 'Please enter a shipping address.' },
   176	        { status: 400 }
   177	      );
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    // Validate phone format
   181	    finalPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(finalPhone);
   182	    if (!isValidPhoneNumber(finalPhone)) {
   183	      return NextResponse.json(
   184	        { error: 'Invalid phone number format.' },
   185	        { status: 400 }
   186	      );
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    // Verify stock availability
   190	    const stockCheck = await verifyStockAvailability(items);
   191	    if (!stockCheck.available) {
   192	      log.warn('Stock verification failed', {
   193	        userId: session?.user?.id || 'guest',
   194	        errors: stockCheck.errors,
   195	        unavailableProductIds: stockCheck.unavailableProductIds,
   196	        items: items.map((i) => ({
   197	          productId: i.productId,
   198	          variantId: i.variantId,
   199	          quantity: i.quantity,
   200	        })),
   201	      });
   202	      return NextResponse.json(
   203	        {
   204	          error: 'Insufficient stock.',
   205	          details: stockCheck.errors,
   206	          unavailableProductIds: stockCheck.unavailableProductIds,
   207	        },
   208	        { status: 400 }
   209	      );
   210	    }
   211	
   212	    // Calculate total and prepare transaction items
   213	    let totalAmount = 0;
   214	    const transactionItems: Array<{
   215	      productId: string;
   216	      variantId?: string;
   217	      quantity: number;
   218	      price: number;
   219	    }> = [];
   220

     2	 * SEO Configuration

     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Get the base URL for the application
     9	 * Uses environment variables with fallback to production URL
    10	 */
    11	export function getBaseUrl(): string {
    12	  // Check if we're on the server side
    13	  if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
    14	    // Server-side: use environment variable or production URL
    15	
    16	    // Priority 1: Use NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL if set (allows dynamic configuration in Vercel)
    17	    const siteUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL;
    18	    if (siteUrl) {
    19	      return siteUrl;
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    // Priority 2: Use NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL when configured.
    23	    const appUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL;
    24	    if (
    25	      appUrl &&
    26	      (process.env.VERCEL_ENV !== 'production' || !appUrl.includes('localhost'))
    27	    ) {
    28	      return appUrl;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    // Priority 3: Use VERCEL_URL for preview or production deployments.
    32	    const vercelUrl = process.env.VERCEL_URL;
    33	    if (vercelUrl && !vercelUrl.includes('localhost')) {
    34	      return `https://${vercelUrl}`;
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    // Fallback for local development.
    38	    return 'http://localhost:3000';
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  // Client-side: use window.location.origin
    42	  return window.location.origin;
    43	}
    44	
    45	/**
    46	 * Construct absolute URL from path
    47	 * @param path - Relative or absolute path
    48	 * @returns Absolute URL
    49	 */
    50	export function getAbsoluteUrl(path: string): string {
    51	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
    52	
    53	  // If path is already absolute, return it
    54	  if (path.startsWith('http://') || path.startsWith('https://')) {
    55	    return path;
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  // Remove leading slash if present to avoid double slashes
    59	  const cleanPath = path.startsWith('/') ? path : `/${path}`;
    60	
    61	  return `${baseUrl}${cleanPath}`;
    62	}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useToastStore, type Toast as ToastType } from '@/store/toast-store';
import AlertV4 from './Alert';

interface ToastItemProps {
  toast: ToastType;
  onRemove: (id: string) => void;
}

function ToastItem({ toast, onRemove }: ToastItemProps) {
  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
  const [isLeaving, setIsLeaving] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Trigger enter animation
    const showTimer = setTimeout(() => setIsVisible(true), 10);

    // Auto-dismiss after duration
    const duration = toast.duration ?? 4000;
    const dismissTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      setIsLeaving(true);
      setTimeout(() => onRemove(toast.id), 300);
    }, duration);

    return () => {
      clearTimeout(showTimer);
      clearTimeout(dismissTimer);
    };
  }, [toast.id, toast.duration, onRemove]);

  const handleClose = () => {
    setIsLeaving(true);
    setTimeout(() => onRemove(toast.id), 300);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`
        transform transition-all duration-300 ease-out
        ${
          isVisible && !isLeaving
            ? 'translate-x-0 opacity-100'
            : '-translate-x-full opacity-0'
        }
      `}
    >
      <AlertV4
        type={toast.type}
        title={toast.title}
        onClose={handleClose}
        variant="soft"
        compact
        className="shadow-lg min-w-[280px] max-w-[380px]"
      >
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
          <span>{toast.message}</span>
          {toast.action && (
            <button
              onClick={() => {
                toast.action?.onClick();
                handleClose();
              }}
              className="self-start text-sm font-medium underline underline-offset-2 hover:no-underline transition-all"
            >
              {toast.action.label}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </AlertV4>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function ToastContainer() {
  const toasts = useToastStore((state) => state.toasts);
  const removeToast = useToastStore((state) => state.removeToast);

  if (toasts.length === 0) return null;
45-export type { StatCardV4Props } from './StatCard';

     7	 * Map of Persian digits to English digits

     9	const persianDigits = ['۰', '۱', '۲', '۳', '۴', '۵', '۶', '۷', '۸', '۹'];
    10	const arabicDigits = ['٠', '١', '٢', '٣', '٤', '٥', '٦', '٧', '٨', '٩'];
    11	
    12	/**
    13	 * Convert Persian/Arabic digits to English digits
    14	 * @param text - Text containing Persian or Arabic digits
    15	 * @returns Text with English digits
    16	 */
    17	export function convertPersianToEnglish(text: string): string {
    18	  if (!text) return text;
    19	
    20	  let result = text;
    21	
    22	  // Convert Persian digits
    23	  persianDigits.forEach((persianDigit, index) => {
    24	    result = result.replace(new RegExp(persianDigit, 'g'), index.toString());
    25	  });
    26	
    27	  // Convert Arabic digits
    28	  arabicDigits.forEach((arabicDigit, index) => {
    29	    result = result.replace(new RegExp(arabicDigit, 'g'), index.toString());
    30	  });
    31	
    32	  return result;
    33	}
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * Check if text contains Persian/Arabic characters
    37	 * @param text - Text to check
    38	 * @returns true if text contains Persian/Arabic characters
    39	 */
    40	export function containsPersianCharacters(text: string): boolean {
    41	  if (!text) return false;
    42	
    43	  // Persian/Arabic Unicode ranges
    44	  const persianPattern =
    45	    /[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF]/;
    46	  return persianPattern.test(text);
    47	}
    48	
    49	/**
    50	 * Validate Persian name (allows Persian letters, spaces, and common Persian characters)
    51	 * @param name - Name to validate
    52	 * @returns true if name is valid Persian name
    53	 */
    54	export function isValidPersianName(name: string): boolean {
    55	  if (!name || !name.trim()) return false;
    56	
    57	  // Allow Persian letters, spaces, Arabic diacritics, and common Persian punctuation
    58	  const persianNamePattern =
    59	    /^[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF\s]+$/;
    60	  return persianNamePattern.test(name.trim());
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * Validate if text can be a valid name (Persian or English)
    65	 * @param name - Name to validate
    66	 * @returns true if name is valid (Persian or English letters)
    67	 */
    68	export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
    69	  if (!name || !name.trim()) return false;
    70	
    71	  // Allow Persian, Arabic, English letters, spaces, hyphens, and apostrophes
    72	  const namePattern =
    73	    /^[\u0600-\u06FF\u0750-\u077F\u08A0-\u08FF\uFB50-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFFa-zA-Z\s'-]+$/;
    74	  return namePattern.test(name.trim());
    75	}
    76	
    77	/**
    78	 * Normalize phone number by converting Persian/Arabic digits to English
    79	 * @param phone - Phone number with potentially Persian/Arabic digits
    80	 * @returns Normalized phone number with English digits
    81	 */
    82	export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
    83	  if (!phone) return phone;
    84	
    85	  // Convert Persian/Arabic digits to English
    86	  const normalized = convertPersianToEnglish(phone);
    87	
    88	  // Remove any non-digit characters except leading +
    89	  return normalized.replace(/[^\d+]/g, '').replace(/\+(?=.)/g, '');
    90	}
    91	
    92	/**
    93	 * Validate Iranian phone number format (09xxxxxxxxx)
    94	 * Accepts both Persian and English digits
    95	 * @param phone - Phone number to validate
    96	 * @returns true if valid Iranian phone format
    97	 */
    98	export function isValidIranianPhone(phone: string): boolean {
    99	  if (!phone) return false;
   100	
   101	  // Normalize first
   102	  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
   103	
   104	  // Check if matches Iranian phone format (09xxxxxxxxx - 11 digits starting with 09)
   105	  return /^09\d{9}$/.test(normalized);
   106	}

    56	export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
    57	  if (!phone) return phone;
    58	
    59	  const defaultCountry = getDefaultPhoneCountry();
    60	  const legacyIranianNumber = getLegacyIranianLocalNumber(phone);
    61	  if (legacyIranianNumber) {
    62	    return legacyIranianNumber;
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  let normalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
    66	
    67	  normalized = normalized.replace(/(?!^)\+/g, '');
    68	  if (normalized.startsWith('00')) {
    69	    normalized = `+${normalized.slice(2)}`;
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  try {
    73	    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
    74	    if (parsed?.isValid()) {
    75	      return parsed.number;
    76	    }
    77	  } catch {
    78	    return normalized;
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  return normalized;
    82	}

    93	    ?.formatNational()

    98	      [
    99	        legacyIranianNumber,
   100	        normalized,
   101	        nationalFormat,
   102	        legacyNormalized,
   103	        legacyWithoutPlus,
   104	      ].filter((candidate): candidate is string => Boolean(candidate))
   105	    )

codex
The patch introduces a phone validation regression that accepts malformed legacy-looking numbers in registration/auth paths. This should be fixed before considering the change correct.

Review comment:

- [P2] Validate legacy phone parses before accepting — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/utils/text.ts:112-113
  When the registration/auth APIs receive an 11-digit value starting with `0` that `libphonenumber-js` can parse but marks invalid, such as `00123456789`, `getLegacyIranianLocalNumber()` still returns a `.number`, so this branch treats it as a valid phone and can store/login with `+123456789`. Check `parsed?.isValid()` before returning/accepting the legacy candidate.
The patch introduces a phone validation regression that accepts malformed legacy-looking numbers in registration/auth paths. This should be fixed before considering the change correct.

Review comment:

- [P2] Validate legacy phone parses before accepting — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/utils/text.ts:112-113
  When the registration/auth APIs receive an 11-digit value starting with `0` that `libphonenumber-js` can parse but marks invalid, such as `00123456789`, `getLegacyIranianLocalNumber()` still returns a `.number`, so this branch treats it as a valid phone and can store/login with `+123456789`. Check `parsed?.isValid()` before returning/accepting the legacy candidate.
